Both the Inch and Centimeter measurement units are supported.\r\n\r\nThe app is capable of creating Code 39, Industrial 2 of 5 and POSTNET barcode using TrueType fonts. This is important for printing high quality barcode labels as it allows high resolution printing and produces barcodes that are sharp and accurate. The high resolution barcodes also ensures requirements of industry specifications such as those by GS1 and ISO can be met with ease. The QR Code 2D barcode is also supported and is generated using a high resolution image.\r\n\r\nThe app is designed to work on both tablet and desktop mode on Windows  and supports users using either the touch or mouse input interface.\r\n \r\nOur Philosophy\r\n\r\nHave you ever thought about how many times you need to use or reuse your barcode and labels?
